Python API Documentation

Notes on API Implementation

Simple Implementation

from browser_engine import WebSimulationRequest

tasks = {
    "task-1": {
        "task_type": "get_screenshot",
        "task_code": ""
    },
    "task-2": {
        "task_type": "get_html",
        "task_code": ""
    }

}
default_browser_settings = {
                        "viewport": "1280x720",
                        "timeout": 180,
                        "load_images": false
                    }

web_request =  WebSimulationRequest(
                    url= "https://invana.io",
                    method="GET",
                    init_headers="",
                    browser_settings=default_browser_settings,
                    tasks=tasks
                )
web_request.run()
